  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=6.8)
    The story avoids most AI pitfalls through specific, unique imagery and consistent characterization. However, certain phrases like "dance on the edge of madness until gravity blushed" and "cool armor" feel overly poetic for the narrator's established voice. Some metaphors, while vivid, occasionally edge into purple prose. The narrative maintains a consistent tone throughout but sometimes relies on elaborate descriptions that, while beautiful, occasionally distance the reader from the character's emotional reality rather than enhancing it.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.4)

== Grader: Qwen 3 235B A22B ==
  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=8.2)
    Vibrant originality in blending genres and surrealism; avoids clichés but occasionally leans on esoteric phrasing over emotional immediacy.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=7.8)
    Writing avoids overt clichés but flirts with "quirky savior" tropes. Emotional beats are shown through imagery rather than stated, though Grotesque's redemption leans on convenient narrative magic rather than human-scale logic.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=7.9)
    World is highly original, avoiding genre tropes through fresh combinations (scarecrow mentor, sentient orchard). However, some phrasing ("shimmering fruit," "blank mercy") verges on generic. Emotional resonance leans on stated reactions ("laughter... equal parts funeral bell and circus calliope") rather than intimate psychological nuance.

  * grade_story_102.txt (grade=6.3)
    Victorian key and cartographic mysticism breathe originality, but "spineless mercenary" and "forgotten trails" recycle archetypes; "luminous doubt" and "hushed prophecy" feel freshly interrogated; overreliance on "lambent" prose risks self-parody; emotional beats often told over shown.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=7.0)
    Some phrases ('cicadas of server rooms') show human-level ingenuity but 'elasticize' and 'quarantined banquets' teeter toward conceptual overwriting.

  * grade_story_106.txt (grade=7.1)
    Some phrases ("unforecast thunder," "coral-claimed statues") innovate clichés, but reliance on alliteration ("erased boundaries," "eccentric cartography") and overabstraction weakens emotional immediacy; inconsistent tonal shifts in final paragraphs.

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=6.1)
    Originality shines in niche concepts (e.g., soul-mirroring seashells), but some elements verge on clichéd (witchy academia, hidden diaries). Prose alternates between lushly poetic and overly technical, with uneven tonal shifts; “frantic peace” feels like an imported buzzword rather than a lived experience.

  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=9.0)
    Originality shines through unexpected juxtapositions (marching bands with architectural anxiety) and metaphors refracted through craft (“maps cryptically obvious”).
